    Under Section 57 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994), the Governor of Tamil
Nadu hereby reserves the offices of the Chairmen of District Panchayats for the persons belonging to the
Scheduled Castes and Scheduled Tribes and for Women as specified in the table below:-

Reservation of the offices of Village Panchayat Presidents for Scheduled Caste, Scheduled 
Tribe and Women
Acharapakkam Panchayat Union
Acharapakkam Panchayat Union Contd...
Kancheepuram District
RESERVATION OF OFFICES OF THE PRESIDENTS OF VILLAGE PANCHAYATS FOR THE PERSONS 
BELONGING TO THE SCHEDULED CASTES AND SCHEDULED TRIBES AND FOR WOMEN UNDER 
TAMIL NADU PANCHAYATS ACT, 1994.
G.O. Ms. No.104, Rural Development and Panchayat Raj (PR-1) Department, Dated:16.09.2016
Mtâ 31, J‹K», ÂUtŸSt® M©L 2047
Under section 57 of the Tamil Nadu Panchayats Act, 1994 (Tamil Nadu Act 21 of 1994),
the Governor of Tamil Nadu hereby reserves the offices of the Presidents of Village Panchayats
for the persons belonging to the Scheduled Castes and Scheduled Tribes and for Women as
specified in the Table below:-
